policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/Deployment/argocd-dex-server:
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  labels:
    app.kubernetes.io/component: dex-server
    app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-dex-server
    app.kubernetes.io/part-of: argocd
  name: argocd-dex-server
  namespace: default
spec:
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-dex-server
  template:
    metadata:
      annotations:
        cluster-autoscaler.kubernetes.io/safe-to-evict: "true"
      labels:
        app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-dex-server
    spec:
      affinity:
        podAntiAffinity:
          preferredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution:
          - podAffinityTerm:
              labelSelector:
                matchLabels:
                  app.kubernetes.io/part-of: argocd
              topologyKey: kubernetes.io/hostname
            weight: 5
      containers:
      - command:
        - /shared/argocd-dex
        - rundex
        env:
        - name: ARGOCD_DEX_SERVER_DISABLE_TLS
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: dexserver.disable.tls
              name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
              optional: true
        image: ghcr.io/dexidp/dex:v2.38.0
        imagePullPolicy: Always
        name: dex
        ports:
        - containerPort: 5556
        - containerPort: 5557
        - containerPort: 5558
        securityContext:
          allowPrivilegeEscalation: false
          capabilities:
            drop:
            - ALL
          readOnlyRootFilesystem: true
          runAsNonRoot: true
          seccompProfile:
            type: RuntimeDefault
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /shared
          name: static-files
        - mountPath: /tmp
          name: dexconfig
        - mountPath: /tls
          name: argocd-dex-server-tls
      initContainers:
      - command:
        - /bin/cp
        - -n
        - /usr/local/bin/argocd
        - /shared/argocd-dex
        image: quay.io/argoproj/argocd:v2.12.0
        imagePullPolicy: Always
        name: copyutil
        securityContext:
          allowPrivilegeEscalation: false
          capabilities:
            drop:
            - ALL
          readOnlyRootFilesystem: true
          runAsNonRoot: true
          seccompProfile:
            type: RuntimeDefault
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /shared
          name: static-files
        - mountPath: /tmp
          name: dexconfig
      serviceAccountName: argocd-dex-server
      volumes:
      - emptyDir: {}
        name: static-files
      - emptyDir: {}
        name: dexconfig
      - name: argocd-dex-server-tls

          items:
          - key: tls.crt
            path: tls.crt
          - key: tls.key
            path: tls.key
          - key: ca.crt
            path: ca.crt
          optional: true

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/Deployment/argocd-notifications-controller:
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  labels:
    app.kubernetes.io/component: notifications-controller
    app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-notifications-controller
    app.kubernetes.io/part-of: argocd
  name: argocd-notifications-controller
  namespace: default
spec:
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-notifications-controller
  strategy:
    type: Recreate
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-notifications-controller
    spec:
      containers:
      - args:
        - /usr/local/bin/argocd-notifications
        env:
        - name: ARGOCD_NOTIFICATIONS_CONTROLLER_LOGFORMAT
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: notificationscontroller.log.format
              name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
              optional: true
        - name: ARGOCD_NOTIFICATIONS_CONTROLLER_LOGLEVEL
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: notificationscontroller.log.level
              name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
              optional: true
        - name: ARGOCD_APPLICATION_NAMESPACES
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: application.namespaces
              name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
              optional: true
        - name: ARGOCD_NOTIFICATION_CONTROLLER_SELF_SERVICE_NOTIFICATION_ENABLED
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: notificationscontroller.selfservice.enabled
              name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
              optional: true
        image: quay.io/argoproj/argocd:v2.12.0
        imagePullPolicy: Always
        livenessProbe:
          tcpSocket:
            port: 9001
        name: argocd-notifications-controller
        securityContext:
          allowPrivilegeEscalation: false
          capabilities:
            drop:
            - ALL
          readOnlyRootFilesystem: true
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /app/config/tls
          name: tls-certs
        - mountPath: /app/config/reposerver/tls
          name: argocd-repo-server-tls
        workingDir: /app
      securityContext:
        runAsNonRoot: true
        seccompProfile:
          type: RuntimeDefault
      serviceAccountName: argocd-notifications-controller
      volumes:
      - configMap:
          name: argocd-tls-certs-cm
        name: tls-certs
      - name: argocd-repo-server-tls
        secret:
          items:
          - key: tls.crt
            path: tls.crt
          - key: tls.key
            path: tls.key
          - key: ca.crt
            path: ca.crt
          optional: true
          secretName: argocd-repo-server-tls

        - name: REDIS_PASSWORD
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              key: auth
              name: argocd-redis
        image: redis:7.0.15-alpine

        name: redis
        ports:
        - containerPort: 6379
        securityContext:
          allowPrivilegeEscalation: false
          capabilities:
            drop:
            - ALL
          readOnlyRootFilesystem: true
      initContainers:
      - command:
        - argocd
        - admin
        - redis-initial-password
        image: quay.io/argoproj/argocd:v2.12.0
        imagePullPolicy: IfNotPresent
        name: secret-init
        securityContext:
          allowPrivilegeEscalation: false
          capabilities:
            drop:
            - ALL
          readOnlyRootFilesystem: true
          runAsNonRoot: true
          seccompProfile:
            type: RuntimeDefault
      securityContext:

        runAsUser: 999
        seccompProfile:
          type: RuntimeDefault

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/Deployment/argocd-dex-server:
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  labels:
    app.kubernetes.io/component: dex-server
    app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-dex-server
    app.kubernetes.io/part-of: argocd
  name: argocd-dex-server
  namespace: default
spec:
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-dex-server
  template:
    metadata:
      annotations:
        cluster-autoscaler.kubernetes.io/safe-to-evict: "true"
      labels:
        app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-dex-server
    spec:
      affinity:
        podAntiAffinity:
          preferredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution:
          - podAffinityTerm:
              labelSelector:
                matchLabels:
                  app.kubernetes.io/part-of: argocd
              topologyKey: kubernetes.io/hostname
            weight: 5
      containers:
      - command:
        - /shared/argocd-dex
        - rundex
        env:
        - name: ARGOCD_DEX_SERVER_DISABLE_TLS
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: dexserver.disable.tls
              name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
              optional: true
        image: ghcr.io/dexidp/dex:v2.37.0
        imagePullPolicy: Always
        name: dex
        ports:
        - containerPort: 5556
        - containerPort: 5557
        - containerPort: 5558
        securityContext:
          allowPrivilegeEscalation: false
          capabilities:
            drop:
            - ALL
          readOnlyRootFilesystem: true
          runAsNonRoot: true
          seccompProfile:
            type: RuntimeDefault
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /shared
          name: static-files
        - mountPath: /tmp
          name: dexconfig
        - mountPath: /tls
          name: argocd-dex-server-tls
      initContainers:
      - command:
        - /bin/cp
        - -n
        - /usr/local/bin/argocd
        - /shared/argocd-dex
        image: quay.io/argoproj/argocd:v2.8.11
        imagePullPolicy: Always
        name: copyutil
        securityContext:
          allowPrivilegeEscalation: false
          capabilities:
            drop:
            - ALL
          readOnlyRootFilesystem: true
          runAsNonRoot: true
          seccompProfile:
            type: RuntimeDefault
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /shared
          name: static-files
        - mountPath: /tmp
          name: dexconfig
      serviceAccountName: argocd-dex-server
      volumes:
      - emptyDir: {}
        name: static-files
      - emptyDir: {}
        name: dexconfig
      - name: argocd-dex-server-tls
        secret:
          items:
          - key: tls.crt
            path: tls.crt
          - key: tls.key
            path: tls.key
          - key: ca.crt
            path: ca.crt
          optional: true
          secretName: argocd-dex-server-tls

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/Deployment/argocd-notifications-controller:
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  labels:
    app.kubernetes.io/component: notifications-controller
    app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-notifications-controller
    app.kubernetes.io/part-of: argocd
  name: argocd-notifications-controller
  namespace: default
spec:
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-notifications-controller
  strategy:
    type: Recreate
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-notifications-controller
    spec:
      containers:
      - args:
        - /usr/local/bin/argocd-notifications
        env:
        - name: ARGOCD_NOTIFICATIONS_CONTROLLER_LOGFORMAT
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: notificationscontroller.log.format
              name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
              optional: true
        - name: ARGOCD_NOTIFICATIONS_CONTROLLER_LOGLEVEL
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: notificationscontroller.log.level
              name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
              optional: true
        - name: ARGOCD_APPLICATION_NAMESPACES
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: application.namespaces
              name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
              optional: true
        image: quay.io/argoproj/argocd:v2.8.11
        imagePullPolicy: Always
        livenessProbe:
          tcpSocket:
            port: 9001
        name: argocd-notifications-controller
        securityContext:
          allowPrivilegeEscalation: false
          capabilities:
            drop:
            - ALL
          readOnlyRootFilesystem: true
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /app/config/tls
          name: tls-certs
        - mountPath: /app/config/reposerver/tls
          name: argocd-repo-server-tls
        workingDir: /app
      securityContext:
        runAsNonRoot: true
        seccompProfile:
          type: RuntimeDefault
      serviceAccountName: argocd-notifications-controller
      volumes:
      - configMap:
          name: argocd-tls-certs-cm
        name: tls-certs
      - name: argocd-repo-server-tls
        secret:
          items:
          - key: tls.crt
            path: tls.crt
          - key: tls.key
            path: tls.key
          - key: ca.crt
            path: ca.crt
          optional: true
          secretName: argocd-repo-server-tls

---

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/Ingress/argocd-ingress:
apiVersion: networking.k8s.io/v1
kind: Ingress
metadata:
  annotations:
    cert-manager.io/cluster-issuer: issuer
    haproxy.org/ssl-passthrough: "true"
  labels:
    app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-ingress
    app.kubernetes.io/part-of: argocd
  name: argocd-ingress
  namespace: default
spec:
  ingressClassName: haproxy
  rules:
  - host: deploy.domain.com
    http:
      paths:
      - backend:
          service:
            name: argocd-server
            port:
              name: https
        path: /
        pathType: Prefix
  tls:
  - hosts:
    - deploy.domain.com
    secretName: argocd-server-tls

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/Ingress/argocd-ingress:
apiVersion: networking.k8s.io/v1
kind: Ingress
metadata:
  annotations:
    cert-manager.io/cluster-issuer: issuer
    haproxy.org/ssl-passthrough: "true"
  labels:
    app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-ingress
    app.kubernetes.io/part-of: argocd
  name: argocd-ingress
  namespace: default
spec:
  ingressClassName: haproxy
  rules:
  - host: deploy.domain.com
    http:
      paths:
      - backend:
          service:
            name: argocd-server
            port:
              name: https
        path: /
        pathType: Prefix
  tls:
  - hosts:
    - deploy.domain.com
    secretName: argocd-server-tls

---

  labels:
    app.kubernetes.io/component: notifications-controller
    app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-notifications-controller
    app.kubernetes.io/part-of: argocd
  name: argocd-notifications-controller
  namespace: default
spec:
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-notifications-controller
  strategy:
    type: Recreate
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-notifications-controller
    spec:
      containers:
      - args:
        - /usr/local/bin/argocd-notifications
        env:
        - name: ARGOCD_NOTIFICATIONS_CONTROLLER_LOGFORMAT
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: notificationscontroller.log.format
              name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
              optional: true
        - name: ARGOCD_NOTIFICATIONS_CONTROLLER_LOGLEVEL
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: notificationscontroller.log.level
              name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
              optional: true
        - name: ARGOCD_APPLICATION_NAMESPACES
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: application.namespaces
              name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
              optional: true
        - name: ARGOCD_NOTIFICATION_CONTROLLER_SELF_SERVICE_NOTIFICATION_ENABLED
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: notificationscontroller.selfservice.enabled
              name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
              optional: true
        image: quay.io/argoproj/argocd:v2.12.1
        imagePullPolicy: IfNotPresent
        livenessProbe:
          tcpSocket:
            port: 9001
        name: argocd-notifications-controller
        securityContext:
          allowPrivilegeEscalation: false
          capabilities:
            drop:
            - ALL
          readOnlyRootFilesystem: true
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /app/config/tls
          name: tls-certs
        - mountPath: /app/config/reposerver/tls
          name: argocd-repo-server-tls
        workingDir: /app
      securityContext:
        runAsNonRoot: true
        seccompProfile:
          type: RuntimeDefault
      serviceAccountName: argocd-notifications-controller
      volumes:
      - configMap:
          name: argocd-tls-certs-cm
        name: tls-certs
      - name: argocd-repo-server-tls
        secret:
          items:
          - key: tls.crt
            path: tls.crt
          - key: tls.key
            path: tls.key
          - key: ca.crt
            path: ca.crt
          optional: true
          secretName: argocd-repo-server-tls

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/Deployment/argocd-dex-server:
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  labels:
    app.kubernetes.io/component: dex-server
    app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-dex-server
    app.kubernetes.io/part-of: argocd
  name: argocd-dex-server
  namespace: default

    matchLabels:
      app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-dex-server

    metadata:
      annotations:
        cluster-autoscaler.kubernetes.io/safe-to-evict: "true"
      labels:
        app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-dex-server
    spec:
      affinity:
        podAntiAffinity:
          preferredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution:
          - podAffinityTerm:
              labelSelector:
                matchLabels:
                  app.kubernetes.io/part-of: argocd
              topologyKey: kubernetes.io/hostname
            weight: 5
      containers:

        - /shared/argocd-dex
        - rundex
        env:
        - name: ARGOCD_DEX_SERVER_DISABLE_TLS
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: dexserver.disable.tls
              name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
              optional: true
        image: ghcr.io/dexidp/dex:v2.37.0
        imagePullPolicy: Always
        name: dex
        ports:
        - containerPort: 5556
        - containerPort: 5557
        - containerPort: 5558
        securityContext:
          allowPrivilegeEscalation: false
          capabilities:
            drop:
            - ALL
          readOnlyRootFilesystem: true
          runAsNonRoot: true
          seccompProfile:
            type: RuntimeDefault
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /shared
          name: static-files
        - mountPath: /tmp
          name: dexconfig
        - mountPath: /tls
          name: argocd-dex-server-tls
      initContainers:
      - command:
        - /bin/cp
        - -n
        - /usr/local/bin/argocd
        - /shared/argocd-dex
        image: quay.io/argoproj/argocd:v2.10.6
        imagePullPolicy: Always
        name: copyutil
        securityContext:
          allowPrivilegeEscalation: false
          capabilities:
            drop:
            - ALL
          readOnlyRootFilesystem: true
          runAsNonRoot: true
          seccompProfile:
            type: RuntimeDefault
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /shared
          name: static-files
        - mountPath: /tmp
          name: dexconfig
      serviceAccountName: argocd-dex-server
      volumes:
      - emptyDir: {}
        name: static-files
      - emptyDir: {}

          - key: tls.key
            path: tls.key
          - key: ca.crt

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/Deployment/argocd-notifications-controller:
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  labels:
    app.kubernetes.io/component: notifications-controller
    app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-notifications-controller
    app.kubernetes.io/part-of: argocd
  name: argocd-notifications-controller
  namespace: default
spec:
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-notifications-controller
  strategy:
    type: Recreate
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-notifications-controller
    spec:
      containers:
      - args:
        - /usr/local/bin/argocd-notifications
        env:
        - name: ARGOCD_NOTIFICATIONS_CONTROLLER_LOGFORMAT
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: notificationscontroller.log.format
              name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
              optional: true
        - name: ARGOCD_NOTIFICATIONS_CONTROLLER_LOGLEVEL
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: notificationscontroller.log.level
              name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
              optional: true
        - name: ARGOCD_APPLICATION_NAMESPACES
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: application.namespaces
              name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
              optional: true
        - name: ARGOCD_NOTIFICATION_CONTROLLER_SELF_SERVICE_NOTIFICATION_ENABLED
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: notificationscontroller.selfservice.enabled
              name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
              optional: true
        image: quay.io/argoproj/argocd:v2.10.6
        imagePullPolicy: Always
        livenessProbe:
          tcpSocket:
            port: 9001
        name: argocd-notifications-controller
        securityContext:
          allowPrivilegeEscalation: false
          capabilities:
            drop:
            - ALL
          readOnlyRootFilesystem: true
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /app/config/tls
          name: tls-certs
        - mountPath: /app/config/reposerver/tls
          name: argocd-repo-server-tls
        workingDir: /app
      securityContext:
        runAsNonRoot: true
        seccompProfile:
          type: RuntimeDefault
      serviceAccountName: argocd-notifications-controller
      volumes:
      - configMap:
          name: argocd-tls-certs-cm
        name: tls-certs
      - name: argocd-repo-server-tls
        secret:
          items:
          - key: tls.crt
            path: tls.crt
          - key: tls.key
            path: tls.key
          - key: ca.crt
            path: ca.crt
          optional: true
          secretName: argocd-repo-server-tls

---

        app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-dex-server

        podAntiAffinity:
          preferredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution:
          - podAffinityTerm:
              labelSelector:

                  app.kubernetes.io/part-of: argocd
              topologyKey: kubernetes.io/hostname

              key: dexserver.disable.tls

              optional: true

        name: dex
        ports:
        - containerPort: 5556
        - containerPort: 5557
        - containerPort: 5558

          allowPrivilegeEscalation: false
          capabilities:
            drop:
            - ALL
          readOnlyRootFilesystem: true
          runAsNonRoot: true
          seccompProfile:
            type: RuntimeDefault
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /shared
          name: static-files
        - mountPath: /tmp
          name: dexconfig
        - mountPath: /tls
          name: argocd-dex-server-tls

      - command:
        - /bin/cp
        - -n
        - /usr/local/bin/argocd
        - /shared/argocd-dex

        imagePullPolicy: Always
        name: copyutil
        securityContext:
          allowPrivilegeEscalation: false
          capabilities:
            drop:
            - ALL
          readOnlyRootFilesystem: true
          runAsNonRoot: true
          seccompProfile:
            type: RuntimeDefault
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /shared
          name: static-files
        - mountPath: /tmp
          name: dexconfig
      serviceAccountName: argocd-dex-server

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/Deployment/argocd-notifications-controller:
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  labels:
    app.kubernetes.io/component: notifications-controller
    app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-notifications-controller
    app.kubernetes.io/part-of: argocd
  name: argocd-notifications-controller
  namespace: default

  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-notifications-controller
  strategy:
    type: Recreate
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-notifications-controller
    spec:
      containers:
      - args:
        - /usr/local/bin/argocd-notifications
        env:
        - name: ARGOCD_NOTIFICATIONS_CONTROLLER_LOGFORMAT
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: notificationscontroller.log.format
              name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
              optional: true
        - name: ARGOCD_NOTIFICATIONS_CONTROLLER_LOGLEVEL
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: notificationscontroller.log.level
              name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
              optional: true
        - name: ARGOCD_APPLICATION_NAMESPACES
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: application.namespaces
              name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
              optional: true
        - name: ARGOCD_NOTIFICATION_CONTROLLER_SELF_SERVICE_NOTIFICATION_ENABLED
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: notificationscontroller.selfservice.enabled
              name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
              optional: true
        image: quay.io/argoproj/argocd:v2.10.6
        imagePullPolicy: Always
        livenessProbe:
          tcpSocket:
            port: 9001
        name: argocd-notifications-controller
        securityContext:
          allowPrivilegeEscalation: false
          capabilities:
            drop:
            - ALL
          readOnlyRootFilesystem: true
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /app/config/tls
          name: tls-certs
        - mountPath: /app/config/reposerver/tls
          name: argocd-repo-server-tls
        workingDir: /app
      securityContext:
        runAsNonRoot: true
        seccompProfile:
          type: RuntimeDefault
      serviceAccountName: argocd-notifications-controller
      volumes:
      - configMap:
          name: argocd-tls-certs-cm
        name: tls-certs
      - name: argocd-repo-server-tls
        secret:
          items:
          - key: tls.crt
            path: tls.crt
          - key: tls.key
            path: tls.key
          - key: ca.crt
            path: ca.crt
          optional: true
          secretName: argocd-repo-server-tls

##### FILE: argocd-cm14.yaml #####

Applying 61 policy rule(s) to 1 resource(s)...

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/ConfigMap/argocd-cm:
apiVersion: v1
data:
  admin.enabled: "false"
  application.resourceTrackingMethod: annotation
  dex.config: |
    connectors:
    - config:
        issuer: https://accounts.google.com
        clientID: <argocd-cm | jsonPath {.clientID}>
        clientSecret: <argocd-cm | jsonPath {.clientSecret}>
      type: oidc
      id: google
      name: Google
  resource.customizations: |
    "*.gcp.upbound.io/*":
      health.lua: |
        hs = {
          status = "Progressing",
          message = "Provisioning ..."
        }


        if obj.status == nil or obj.status.conditions == nil then
          return hs
        end

        for i, condition in ipairs(obj.status.conditions) do
          if condition.type == "LastAsyncOperation" then
            if condition.status == "False" then
              hs.status = "Degraded"
              hs.message = condition.message
              return hs
            end
          end

          if condition.type == "Synced" then
            if condition.status == "False" then
              hs.status = "Degraded"
              hs.message = condition.message
              return hs
            end
          end

          if condition.type == "Ready" then
            if condition.status == "True" then
              hs.status = "Healthy"
              hs.message = "Resource is up-to-date."
              return hs
            end
          end
        end

        return hs
  resource.customizations.ignoreDifferences.all: |
    jqPathExpressions:
      - .spec.template.spec.initContainers[].resources
      - .spec.template.spec.containers[].resources
  resource.customizations.ignoreDifferences.cilium.io_CiliumClusterwideNetworkPolicy: |
    jsonPointers:
      - "/status"
  statusbadge.enabled: "true"
  url: https://argocd.ys7.me
  users.anonymous.enabled: "false"
kind: ConfigMap
metadata:
  annotations:
    avp.kubernetes.io/path: projects/dev-infra/secrets/argocd-cm
  name: argocd-cm
  namespace: default

---

##### FILE: argocd-cmd-params-cm15.yaml #####

Applying 61 policy rule(s) to 1 resource(s)...

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/ConfigMap/argocd-cmd-params-cm:
apiVersion: v1
data:
  application.resourceTrackingMethod: annotation
  resource.customizations: |
    "*.upbound.io/*":
      health.lua: |
        health_status = {
          status = "Progressing",
          message = "Provisioning ..."
        }

        local function contains (table, val)
          for i, v in ipairs(table) do
            if v == val then
              return true
            end
          end
          return false
        end

        local has_no_status = {
          "ProviderConfig",
          "ProviderConfigUsage"
        }

        if obj.status == nil and contains(has_no_status, obj.kind) then
          health_status.status = "Healthy"
          health_status.message = "Resource is up-to-date."
          return health_status
        end

        if obj.status == nil or obj.status.conditions == nil then
          if obj.kind == "ProviderConfig" and obj.status.users ~= nil then
            health_status.status = "Healthy"
            health_status.message = "Resource is in use."
            return health_status
          end
          return health_status
        end

        for i, condition in ipairs(obj.status.conditions) do
          if condition.type == "LastAsyncOperation" then
            if condition.status == "False" then
              health_status.status = "Degraded"
              health_status.message = condition.message
              return health_status
            end
          end

          if condition.type == "Synced" then
            if condition.status == "False" then
              health_status.status = "Degraded"
              health_status.message = condition.message
              return health_status
            end
          end

          if condition.type == "Ready" then
            if condition.status == "True" then
              health_status.status = "Healthy"
              health_status.message = "Resource is up-to-date."
              return health_status
            end
          end
        end

        return health_status

    "*.crossplane.io/*":
      health.lua: |
        health_status = {
          status = "Progressing",
          message = "Provisioning ..."
        }

        local function contains (table, val)
          for i, v in ipairs(table) do
            if v == val then
              return true
            end
          end
          return false
        end

        local has_no_status = {
          "Composition",
          "CompositionRevision",
          "DeploymentRuntimeConfig",
          "ControllerConfig"
        }
        if obj.status == nil and contains(has_no_status, obj.kind) then
            health_status.status = "Healthy"
            health_status.message = "Resource is up-to-date."
          return health_status
        end

        if obj.status == nil or obj.status.conditions == nil then
          return health_status
        end

        for i, condition in ipairs(obj.status.conditions) do
          if condition.type == "LastAsyncOperation" then
            if condition.status == "False" then
              health_status.status = "Degraded"
              health_status.message = condition.message
              return health_status
            end
          end

          if condition.type == "Synced" then
            if condition.status == "False" then
              health_status.status = "Degraded"
              health_status.message = condition.message
              return health_status
            end
          end

          if contains({"Ready", "Healthy", "Offered", "Established"}, condition.type) then
            if condition.status == "True" then
              health_status.status = "Healthy"
              health_status.message = "Resource is up-to-date."
              return health_status
            end
          end
        end

        return health_status
  resource.exlusions: |
    - apiGroups:
      - "*"
      kinds:
      - ProviderConfigUsage
  server.insecure: "true"
kind: ConfigMap
metadata:
  labels:
    app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
    app.kubernetes.io/part-of: argocd
  name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
  namespace: default

---

apiVersion: networking.k8s.io/v1
kind: Ingress
metadata:
  annotations:
    cert-manager.io/cluster-issuer: letsencrypt-prod
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/backend-protocol: HTTPS
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/ssl-passthrough: "true"
  name: argocd-server-ingress
  namespace: argocd
spec:
  ingressClassName: nginx
  rules:
  - host: argocd.happycloudcomputing.com

      paths:

          service:
            name: argocd-server
            port:
              name: https
        path: /
        pathType: Prefix
  tls:
  - hosts:
    - argocd.happycloudcomputing.com

##### FILE: argocd-notifications-controller-deployment.yaml #####

Applying 61 policy rule(s) to 1 resource(s)...

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/Deployment/argocd-notifications-controller:
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  labels:
    app.kubernetes.io/component: notifications-controller
    app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-notifications-controller
    app.kubernetes.io/part-of: argocd
  name: argocd-notifications-controller
  namespace: default
spec:
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-notifications-controller
  strategy:
    type: Recreate
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-notifications-controller
    spec:
      containers:
      - args:
        - /usr/local/bin/argocd-notifications
        env:
        - name: ARGOCD_NOTIFICATIONS_CONTROLLER_LOGFORMAT
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: notificationscontroller.log.format
              name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
              optional: true
        - name: ARGOCD_NOTIFICATIONS_CONTROLLER_LOGLEVEL
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: notificationscontroller.log.level
              name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
              optional: true
        - name: ARGOCD_APPLICATION_NAMESPACES
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: application.namespaces
              name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
              optional: true
        - name: ARGOCD_NOTIFICATION_CONTROLLER_SELF_SERVICE_NOTIFICATION_ENABLED
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: notificationscontroller.selfservice.enabled
              name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
              optional: true
        - name: ARGOCD_NOTIFICATION_CONTROLLER_REPO_SERVER_PLAINTEXT
          valueFrom:
            configMapKeyRef:
              key: notificationscontroller.repo.server.plaintext
              name: argocd-cmd-params-cm
              optional: true
        image: quay.io/argoproj/argocd:latest
        imagePullPolicy: Always
        livenessProbe:
          tcpSocket:
            port: 9001
        name: argocd-notifications-controller
        securityContext:
          allowPrivilegeEscalation: false
          capabilities:
            drop:
            - ALL
          readOnlyRootFilesystem: true
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /app/config/tls
          name: tls-certs
        - mountPath: /app/config/reposerver/tls
          name: argocd-repo-server-tls
        workingDir: /app
      securityContext:
        runAsNonRoot: true
        seccompProfile:
          type: RuntimeDefault
      serviceAccountName: argocd-notifications-controller
      volumes:
      - configMap:
          name: argocd-tls-certs-cm
        name: tls-certs
      - name: argocd-repo-server-tls
        secret:
          items:
          - key: tls.crt
            path: tls.crt
          - key: tls.key
            path: tls.key
          - key: ca.crt
            path: ca.crt
          optional: true
          secretName: argocd-repo-server-tls

---


Mutation:
Mutation has been applied successfully.

##### FILE: argocd-redis-deployment.yaml #####

Applying 61 policy rule(s) to 1 resource(s)...

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/Deployment/argocd-redis:
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  labels:
    app.kubernetes.io/component: redis
    app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-redis
    app.kubernetes.io/part-of: argocd
  name: argocd-redis
  namespace: default
spec:
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-redis
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-redis
    spec:
      affinity:
        podAntiAffinity:
          preferredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution:
          - podAffinityTerm:
              labelSelector:
                matchLabels:
                  app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-redis
              topologyKey: kubernetes.io/hostname
            weight: 100
          - podAffinityTerm:
              labelSelector:
                matchLabels:
                  app.kubernetes.io/part-of: argocd
              topologyKey: kubernetes.io/hostname
            weight: 5
      containers:
      - args:
        - --save
        - ""
        - --appendonly
        - "no"
        - --requirepass $(REDIS_PASSWORD)
        env:
        - name: REDIS_PASSWORD
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              key: auth
              name: argocd-redis
        image: redis:7.0.15-alpine
        imagePullPolicy: Always
        name: redis
        ports:
        - containerPort: 6379
        securityContext:
          allowPrivilegeEscalation: false
          capabilities:
            drop:
            - ALL
          readOnlyRootFilesystem: true
      initContainers:
      - command:
        - argocd
        - admin
        - redis-initial-password
        image: quay.io/argoproj/argocd:latest
        imagePullPolicy: IfNotPresent
        name: secret-init
        securityContext:
          allowPrivilegeEscalation: false
          capabilities:
            drop:
            - ALL
          readOnlyRootFilesystem: true
          runAsNonRoot: true
          seccompProfile:
            type: RuntimeDefault
      securityContext:
        runAsNonRoot: true
        runAsUser: 999
        seccompProfile:
          type: RuntimeDefault
      serviceAccountName: argocd-redis

---

          subPath: docker-credential-gcr

          name: docker-config
          readOnly: true
      - command:
        - /var/run/argocd/argocd-cmp-server
        image: busybox:1.36
        name: cue-plugin
        resources:
          limits:
            cpu: 4
            memory: 4Gi
          requests:
            cpu: 4
            memory: 4Gi
        securityContext:
          runAsNonRoot: true
          runAsUser: 999
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /var/run/argocd
          name: var-files
        - mountPath: /home/argocd/cmp-server/plugins
          name: plugins
        - mountPath: /home/argocd/cmp-server/config/plugin.yaml
          name: cue-plugin
          subPath: plugin.yaml
        - mountPath: /usr/local/bin/cue
          name: tools
          subPath: cue
        - mountPath: /tmp
          name: cmp-tmp
      - command:
        - /var/run/argocd/argocd-cmp-server
        env:
        - name: AVP_TYPE
          value: gcpsecretmanager
        image: quay.io/argoproj/argocd:v2.11.0
        name: argocd-vault-plugin
        resources:
          limits:
            cpu: 500m
            memory: 2Gi
          requests:
            cpu: 500m
            memory: 2Gi
        securityContext:
          runAsNonRoot: true
          runAsUser: 999
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /var/run/argocd
          name: var-files
        - mountPath: /home/argocd/cmp-server/plugins
          name: plugins
        - mountPath: /home/argocd/cmp-server/config/plugin.yaml
          name: argocd-vault-plugin
          subPath: plugin.yaml
        - mountPath: /usr/local/bin/argocd-vault-plugin
          name: tools
          subPath: argocd-vault-plugin
        - mountPath: /tmp
          name: cmp-tmp
      initContainers:
      - command:
        - sh
        - -c
        - "wget https://github.com/cue-lang/cue/releases/download/v$(CUE_VERSION)/cue_v$(CUE_VERSION)_linux_amd64.tar.gz
          -O - | tar -xz && \nchmod +x cue && mv cue /tools/cue\n\nwget https://github.com/argoproj-labs/argocd-vault-plugin/releases/download/v$(AVP_VERSION)/argocd-vault-plugin_$(AVP_VERSION)_linux_amd64
          -O argocd-vault-plugin &&\nchmod +x argocd-vault-plugin && mv argocd-vault-plugin
          /tools/argocd-vault-plugin\n\nwget https://github.com/GoogleCloudPlatform/docker-credential-gcr/releases/download/v$(GCR_VERSION)/docker-credential-gcr_linux_amd64-$(GCR_VERSION).tar.gz
          -O - | tar -xz &&\nchmod +x docker-credential-gcr && mv docker-credential-gcr
          /var/run/docker-credential-gcr/docker-credential-gcr\nPATH=/var/run/docker-credential-gcr/:$PATH
          HOME=/var/run/config docker-credential-gcr configure-docker --include-artifact-registry\nchmod
          +r /var/run/config/.docker/config.json\n"
        env:
        - name: CUE_VERSION
          value: 0.8.2
        - name: AVP_VERSION
          value: 1.17.0
        - name: GCR_VERSION
          value: 2.1.22
        image: busybox:1.36
        name: toolchain-setup
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /tools
          name: tools
        - mountPath: /var/run/docker-credential-gcr
          name: docker-credential-gcr
        - mountPath: /var/run/config/.docker

          name: cue-plugin
        name: cue-plugin

          name: argocd-vault-plugin
        name: argocd-vault-plugin
      - emptyDir: {}
        name: cmp-tmp
      - emptyDir: {}
        name: tools
      - emptyDir: {}
        name: docker-credential-gcr
      - emptyDir: {}
        name: docker-config

apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: argocd-repo-server
  namespace: default
spec:
  replicas: 2
  template:
    spec:
      affinity:
        podAntiAffinity:
          preferredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution:
          - podAffinityTerm:
              labelSelector:
                matchLabels:
                  app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-repo-server
              topologyKey: topology.kubernetes.io/zone
            weight: 100
          requiredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution:
          - labelSelector:
              matchLabels:
                app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-repo-server
            topologyKey: kubernetes.io/hostname
      containers:
      - args:
        - /usr/local/bin/argocd-repo-server
        name: argocd-repo-server

##### FILE: argocd-repo-server-deployment-patch.yaml #####

Applying 61 policy rule(s) to 1 resource(s)...

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/Deployment/argocd-repo-server:
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: argocd-repo-server
  namespace: default
spec:
  template:
    metadata:
      annotations:
        cluster-autoscaler.kubernetes.io/safe-to-evict: "true"
    spec:
      containers:
      - args:
        - --loglevel
        - debug
        command:
        - /var/run/argocd/argocd-cmp-server
        image: busybox
        name: helm-plugin
        securityContext:
          runAsNonRoot: true
          runAsUser: 999
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /var/run/argocd
          name: var-files
        - mountPath: /home/argocd/cmp-server/plugins
          name: plugins
        - mountPath: /helm-working-dir
          name: helm-plugin-tmp
        - mountPath: /home/argocd/cmp-server/config/plugin.yaml
          name: helm-plugin-config
          subPath: plugin.yaml
        - mountPath: /var/run/argocd/helm-plugin/generate.sh
          name: helm-plugin-config
          subPath: generate.sh
        - mountPath: /var/run/argocd/helm-plugin/get-parameters.sh
          name: helm-plugin-config
          subPath: get-parameters.sh
        - mountPath: /usr/local/bin
          name: helm-plugin-tools
      initContainers:
      - command:
        - sh
        - -c
        - |
          wget https://get.helm.sh/helm-v3.10.3-linux-amd64.tar.gz -O - | tar xz && mv linux-amd64/helm /tools/helm && chmod +x /tools/helm
          wget https://github.com/stedolan/jq/releases/download/jq-1.6/jq-linux64 -O /tools/jq && chmod +x /tools/jq
          wget https://github.com/mikefarah/yq/releases/download/v4.30.6/yq_linux_amd64 -O /tools/yq && chmod +x /tools/yq
        image: busybox
        name: helm-plugin-setup
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /tools
          name: helm-plugin-tools
      volumes:
      - configMap:
          name: helm-plugin-config
        name: helm-plugin-config
      - emptyDir: {}
        name: helm-plugin-tmp
      - emptyDir: {}
        name: helm-plugin-tools

---

apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: argocd-repo-server
  namespace: default
spec:
  template:
    metadata:
      annotations:
        cluster-autoscaler.kubernetes.io/safe-to-evict: "true"
    spec:
      containers:
      - command:
        - /var/run/argocd/argocd-cmp-server
        - --loglevel=info
        image: busybox:1.36
        name: cuelang-plugin
        securityContext:
          runAsNonRoot: true
          runAsUser: 999
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /var/run/argocd
          name: var-files
        - mountPath: /home/argocd/cmp-server/plugins
          name: plugins
        - mountPath: /cue-working-dir
          name: cmp-plugin-tmp
        - mountPath: /home/argocd/cmp-server/config/plugin.yaml
          name: cue-plugin-config
          subPath: plugin.yaml
        - mountPath: /usr/local/bin
          name: cue-plugin-bin
      initContainers:
      - command:
        - sh
        - -c
        - |
          mv /code/argocue /usr/local/bin/argocue && chmod a+x /usr/local/bin/argocue
          /var/run/install_deps.sh
        image: darkwind8/argocue:v0.4.0
        name: cuelang-plugin-setup
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /usr/local/bin
          name: cue-plugin-bin
        - mountPath: /var/run/install_deps.sh
          name: cue-plugin-config
          subPath: install_deps.sh
      volumes:
      - emptyDir: {}
        name: cue-plugin-bin
      - emptyDir: {}
        name: cmp-plugin-tmp
      - configMap:
          defaultMode: 511
          name: cue-plugin-config
        name: cue-plugin-config

apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment

  namespace: default

          subPath: .gnupg

        - /deploy-key/deploy-key-private
        env:
        - name: GNUPGHOME

        name: import-gpg-key
        volumeMounts:
        - mountPath: /deploy-key
          name: deploy-key
          readOnly: true
        - mountPath: /gpg-home
          name: gpg-home
      volumes:
      - emptyDir: {}
        name: gpg-home
      - name: deploy-key
        secret:
          secretName: argocd-secret

##### FILE: argocd-server-deployment1.yaml #####

Applying 61 policy rule(s) to 1 resource(s)...

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to default/Deployment/argocd-server:
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: argocd-server
  namespace: default
spec:
  replicas: 2
  template:
    spec:
      affinity:
        podAntiAffinity:
          preferredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution:
          - podAffinityTerm:
              labelSelector:
                matchLabels:
                  app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-server
              topologyKey: topology.kubernetes.io/zone
            weight: 100
          requiredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution:
          - labelSelector:
              matchLabels:
                app.kubernetes.io/name: argocd-server
            topologyKey: kubernetes.io/hostname
      containers:
      - args:
        - /usr/local/bin/argocd-server
        env:
        - name: ARGOCD_API_SERVER_REPLICAS
          value: "2"
        name: argocd-server
